# My arXiv Daily

Daily arXiv papers for dexterous manipulation, robot learning, and embodied AI.

Updated on **2026-07-19**.

## Topics

- [Dexterous Hand](#dexterous-hand) (193)
- [Manipulation](#manipulation) (456)
- [Reinforcement Learning](#reinforcement-learning) (602)

- [Tactile / Visuo-Tactile](#tactile--visuo-tactile) (166)
- [Embodied Foundation Models](#embodied-foundation-models) (672)

## Metadata Note

Corresponding author is approximated as the last author from arXiv metadata unless manually curated. Keywords are extracted from each paper title and abstract with a domain vocabulary. The code column is a conservative best-effort GitHub lookup and may be blank when no likely official repository is found.
